| [`2192`](https://decodeunicode.org/U+2192) | `→` | `->` |  |

| [`2225`](https://decodeunicode.org/U+2225) | `∥` | `\|\|` |  |
| [`2261`](https://decodeunicode.org/U+2261) | `≡` | `==` |  |

| [`2A7E`](https://decodeunicode.org/U+2A7E) | `⩾` | `>=` | GREATER-THAN OR SLANTED EQUAL TO |
